Jamison Brereton

64 (890)
All Gods
Gaya Pl─Бta
17 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 12, 16тАУ17
Making up for his restrained focus on the ─Аdityas in the preceding All God hymn (X.63), the poet Gaya Pl─Бta here produces an expansive litany of almost every god and goddess he can think of, major or minor. He begins with rhetorical questions (vs. 1): which god would it be best to address? Having suggested that all of them are potentially his targets (vs. 2), he runs through a long list of possible individuals (vss. 3тАУ12), sometimes listing the bare name, sometimes offering further characterization.
Only in verses 13тАУ14 do we reach something more interesting. In verse 13 he expresses his hope that the Maruts will recognize their тАЬcommon birthтАЭ with him, presumably on the basis of their shared role as singers and poets (on this see also I.87.5), as they meet at the тАЬnavelтАЭ (the loaded word of X.61тАУ62, hymns attrib
uted to a different poet). The navel here must be both the sacrificial ground of the here-and-now and the mythical point of their joint origin, before their division into mortals and gods. In verse 14 he suggests Heaven and Earth as a model for this kin ship. Perhaps the idea is that Heaven and Earth are not divided, with Heaven taking the godsтАЩ side and Earth that of mortals, but they work as partnersтАФboth being related to the gods and both accepting the sacrifice of men. In any case the kinship that the poet has suggested he has with the Maruts as poets he asserts in another way in verse 16, where he describes himself as a тАЬpowerfully roaring poetтАЭ (kav├нs tuv─лr├бv─Бn), the exact phrase with which he identified Br╠еhaspati, the wordsmith par excellence of the gods, in verse 4.
The final two verses (16тАУ17), in a different meter from the rest of the poem, are the poetтАЩs summary verses, both beginning with ev─Б╠Б тАЬin this wayтАЭ and both men tioning the poet by name. The second of the two is also found at the end of X.63.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬIn what manner, and of which of the gods, who hear (our praises) at the sacrifice, may we enunciatethe venerable name? Who will show us compassion? Which of them will grant us happiness? Which of themcomes for our protection?тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Compassion: mс╣Ыс╕╖atirupaday─Бkarm─Б: Nirukta 10.15

Jamison Brereton

How shall we contemplateтАФof which one of the gods shall we
contemplate the name that is good to contemplate, as they listen to
my plea?
Who will be merciful; which one will create joy for us? Which one will turn hither with help?

Griffith

WHAT God, of those who hear, is he whose well-praised name we may record in this our sacrifice; and how?
Who will be gracious? Who of many give us bliss? Who out of all the Host will come to lend us aid?

Wie und an wessen gerngedachten Namen der G├╢tter, die auf der Fahrt erh├╢ren, sollen wir gedenken? Wer wird sich erbarmen, welcher unter den vielen wird uns Freude machen? Welcher wird gn├дdig herlenken?

English translation:

тАЬThe desires cherished in my heart strive to offer worship; (our) wishes long for (the gods) andexpressed (by us) go forth to (the gods); no other bestower of happiness exists except them; upon the gods aremy desire concentrated.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Our intentions are intent (on them), the insights in our hearts. Our trackers follow their track and fly to (all) directions.
No dispenser of mercy other than them is found. My desires have
fastened upon the gods.

Griffith

The will and thoughts within my breast exert their power: they yearn with love, and fly to all the regions round.
None other comforter is found save only these: my longings and my hopes are fixt upon the Gods.

Es erw├дgen im Herzen die Erw├дgungen, die Gedanken; die sp├дhenden Augen des Geistes sp├дhen, sie fliegen nach allen Seiten. Es findet sich kein anderer Erbarmer au├Яer ihnen. Auf die G├╢tter sind meine W├╝nsche gerichtet.

Grassmann

Stark sind die Kr├дfte, in den Herzen hoher Sinn; hold sind die holden, fliegen hin in alle Welt; Kein andrer Tr├╢ster ausser ihnen findet sich, nur zu den G├╢ttern streben meine W├╝nsche hin.

To Narasamsa and to Pusan I sing forth, unconcealable Agni kindied by the Gods.
To Sun and Moon, two Moons, to Yama in the heaven, to Trita, Vata, Dawn, Night, and the Atvins Twain.

Geldner

Soll ich vielleicht den Narasamsa, den Pusan, den Agohya, den von den G├╢ttern entflammten Agni mit meiner Rede preisen, Sonne und Mond, die beiden Monde, Yama im Himmel, den Trita, Vata, die Usas, die Nacht, die Asvin?

English translation:

тАЬHow is the sage(Agni) adored by multitudes, and by what praises? Bс╣Ыhaspati is magnified with sacredhymns; Aja, walking alone, is magnified with solemn invocations and prayers; may Ahirbudhnya hear us at theseason of invocation.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Ahirbudhnya: ahiс╕е budhnyaс╕е, the deep dragon

Jamison Brereton

How will the powerfully roaring poet Br╠еhaspati grow strong, through what hymn with its well-twisted (ornaments)?
Let Aja Ekap─Бd with the chanters who are easy to call, let Ahi Budhnya harken to my call.

Griffith

How is the Sage extolled whom the loud singers praise? What voice, what hymn is used to laud Brhaspati?
May Aja-Ekapad with Rkvans swift to hear, and Ahi of the Deep listen unto our call.

Geldner

Grassmann

Wie wird der weise, rauschende, mit welchem Lied Brihaspati erquickt, mit welchem Opferwerk? Der Kreiselwind, umjubelt von der S├дngerschar, der Wetterdrache h├╢re nun auf unsern Ruf.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬAt the birth of Dakс╣гa, at his sacred rite, you, Aditi, worshipped the royal Mitra and Varuс╣Зa at thesacred rite. Aryaman, whose course is not hurried, the giver of delight to many, having seven ministering (rays),(proceeds) in his multiform births.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Dakс╣гa = the sun;

Aryaman = the sun;

Aditi = earth (Nirukta 11.23); havingsix seasons, and the intercalary month; his multiform births: i.e., his daily risings and settings

Jamison Brereton

Or, o Aditi, at the birth of the skillful one [=Agni] under your
commandment, will you seek to entice here the two kings Mitra and Varuс╣Зa?
(Or will it be) Aryaman, whose path is not to be transgressed, who
possesses many chariots, who possesses seven Hotars, at his births in diverse forms?

Griffith

Aditi, to the birth of Daksa and the vow thou summonest the Kings Mitra and Varuna.
With course unchecked, with many chariots Aryaman comes with the seven priests to tribes of varied sort.

Geldner

Oder vielleicht bittest du, Aditi, bei der Geburt und dem Walten des Daksa, die beiden K├╢nige Mitra und Varuna her. Aryaman, der seinen Weg noch nicht zur├╝ckgelegt hat, der viele Wagen, sieben Opferpriester hat in den verschiedenen Geburten.

Grassmann

Zu Dakscha’s Pflege und Geburt, o Aditi, rufst du die Herrscher Mitra-Varuna herbei; Mit vielen Wagen unverwehrt kommt Arjaman mit sieben Priestern zu ungleichen St├дmmen hin.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay those universal horses (of the deities), who listen to invocations, who are vigorous, swiftroadsters, hear our summons; they who spontaneously are the givers of thousands, as if at sacrifice; they whohave won great wealth in battles.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

As if at sacrifice: medhas─Бt─Бv iva tvaman─Б = medhas─Бt─Б saniс╣гyavaс╕е =desiring to give in the hall of sacrifice (Yajus. 9.17); ahavarvai mitro r─Бtrirvaruс╣Зaс╕е: Aitareya Br─Бhmaс╣Зa 4.10

Jamison Brereton

Let the steeds who heed the call heed our callтАФall the prizewinners of measured pace,
who by themselves win thousands as if at the winning of wisdom, the ones who have greatly borne away for themselves the spoils in the
encounters.

Griffith

May all those vigorous Coursers listen to our cry, hearers of invocation, speeding on their way;
Winners of thousands where the priestly meed is won, who gather of themselves great wealth in every race.

Geldner

Die Rennpferde, die den Anruf erh├╢ren, sollen alle den Ruf h├╢ren, die siegreichen mit festem Schritt, die Tausend gewinnen, wie bei dem Kampf um die Dichtermeisterschaft selbst, die den gro├Яen Siegespreis in den K├дmpfen davongetragen haben.

Grassmann

Die raschen Renner m├╢gen h├╢ren unsern Ruf, die Ruferh├╢rer alle sie, die kr├дftigen, Die tausendfaches nehmen bei dem Opferfest, und grosses Gut erbeuteten in jeder Schlacht.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬImportune, (worshippers), with praises, V─Бyu, harnessing his chariot, and Purandhi and P┼лс╣гan fortheir friendship, for these considerate and consentient deities, attend the sacrifice upon the birth of Savit─Б.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Set in front with your praises V─Бyu, who hitches up the chariot,
Plenitude, and P┼лс╣гan, for comradeship,
for at the impulsion of god Savitar they follow his willтАФthose of one mind (follow the will) of him who is of one mind (with them).

Griffith

Bring ye Purandbi, bring Vayu who yokes his steeds, for friendship bring ye Pusan with your songs of praise:
They with one mind, one thought attend the sacrifice, urged by the favouring aid of Savitar the God.

Geldner

Gebet mit euren Lobpreisungen dem wagenschirrenden Vayu, der Purandhi, dem Pusan zur Freundschaft den Vorzug, denn diese folgen auf Gott Savitri┬┤s Gehei├Я seinem Willen, gleichdenkend, gleichgesinnt!

Grassmann

Den Wagenschirrer Vaju und Purandhi schafft durch Loblied und zur Freundschaft Puschan euch herbei; An Einsicht und an Weisheit gleich erlangen sie auf Savitars, des Gottes, Antrieb neue Kraft.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬWe invoke for protection the thrice seven flowing rivers, (their) great waters, the trees, the mountains,Agni, Kс╣Ы┼Ы─Бnu, the archers, and Tiс╣гya, to the assembly; (we invoke) Rudra, worthy of the praise of the Rudras,for the good of the praisers.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Kс╣Ы┼Ы─Бnu: the gandharva so named; the archers are the gandharvas accompanyinghim; they are the guardians, of the Soma;

Tiс╣гya: nakс╣гatra, a heavenly-archer like Kс╣Ы┼Ы─Бnu? some of the otherthe praisers: among the Rudras

Jamison Brereton

mountains, and Agni do we call upon for helpтАФ

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬplural asant of aspect (is troop of Maruts), like a house well stored with provisions; fortunate is the favourof the Maruts, the sons of Rudra; may we (thereby) be famed among men for cattle, and so, gods, ever approach(you) with sacrificial food.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Delightful to the sight like a peaceful dwelling abounding in food. Auspicious is the praise invocation of the Rudras, the Maruts.
May we be glorious among the peoples with our cows. May we always be accompanied by refreshment, o gods.

Griffith

Pleasant to look on as a dwelling rich in food is the blest favour of the Maruts, Rudra’s Sons.
May we be famed among the folk for wealth in kine. and ever come to you, ye Gods, with sacred food.

Geldner

Erfreulich wie ein nahrungsreiches Haus f├╝r den Anblick, gl├╝ckbringend ist die Lobpreisung der Rudras├╢hne, der Marut. Durch Rinderbesitz wollen wir bei den Leuten angesehn sein. Immerdar m├╢chten wir mit der Ila zusammen sein, o G├╢tter!

Grassmann

Zum Anschaun lieblich wie ein nahrungsreicher Sitz, gl├╝ckbringend ist der pr├дcht’gen Maruts Beifall uns; Durch Heerden seien herrlich unter Menschen wir, stets sein, o G├╢tter, wir mit Labetrunk versorgt.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMaruts, repeatedly acknowledge us, so that (you may make us the objects) of this relationship; andmay Aditi grant us affinity (with men) on the navel of the earth, where we first assemble (to offer oblations).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Surely in some way you will take notice of this common birth of ours, Maruts?
At the navel where we first come together, there let Aditi establish our relationship.

Griffith

O Maruts, do ye never, never recollect and call again to mind this our relationship?
When next we meet together at the central point, even there shall Aditi confirm our brotherhood.

Geldner

Ganz gewi├Я werdet ihr Marut euch irgendwie dieser unserer Bekanntschaft erinnern. An dem Nabel, an dem wir uns zuerst zusammenfanden, an dem soll Aditi unsere Freundschaft wieder herstellen.

Grassmann

Wie ist es denn? o Maruts achtet nimmer ihr auf diese Stammverwandtschaft zwischen uns und euch? Im Heiligthum, wo wir zuerst uns liebend nahn, da setze die Verwandtschaft Aditi uns fest.

English translation:

тАЬThey, two, the maternal heaven and earth, mighty, divine, adorable, attain to the gods upon their birth;they both cherish the two (races, human and divine) (gods), they shed abundant moisture.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

For Heaven and Earth, the two great mothers, the goddesses worthy of the sacrifice, proceed by virtue of their kinship with the gods.
Both support both (breeds [=gods and men]) with their supports, and with the Fathers they sprinkle much seed.

Griffith

The Mothers, Heaven and Earth, those mighty Goddesses, worthy of sacrifice, ecune with the race of Gods.
These Two with their support uphold both Gods and men, and with the Fathers pour the copious genial stream.

Grassmann

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe pious sage, Gaya, eloquent in laudation, conversant with sacred rites, wishing for wealth, eagerfor wealth, propitiates the celestial people with prayers and praises.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

In just this way the powerfully roaring poet, knowing the truth, seeking goods, desiring goods,
the inspired Gaya here with hymns and compositions has swelled the divine races.

Griffith

Thus hath the sage, skilled in loud singers’ duties, desiring riches, yearning after treasure,
Gaya, the priestly singer, with his praises and hymns contented the Celestial people.

Geldner

Also hat der stimmstarke Seher, der Wahrheitskundige, Reichtum begehrend, Reichtum liebend, der redekundige Gaya hier mit seinen Lobliedern und mit Gebeten die himmlischen Geschlechter erf├╝llt.

Grassmann

So hat der weise S├дnger, opferkundig, nach Gut verlangend und des Guts sich freuend Mit Spr├╝chen und Gebeten laut ert├╢nend, Gaja getr├дnkt die himmlischen Geschlechter.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬUniversal deities and Aditi, thus has the prudent son of plural ti magnified you; the celestial people, theimmortal (company of the gods) through whom (when praised) men become the bonds (of wealth), have beenglorified by Gaya.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

In just this way has the son of Plati of inspired thought strengthened you, all you ─Аdityas and Aditi.
The overmastering superior men, the divine race, has been praised by Amartya Gaya.
Hymns X.65тАУ66 are attributed to a Vasukarс╣Зa V─Бsukra, who is otherwise unknown in the R╠еgveda. But his patronymic links him to Vasukra Aindra, poet of the fiend ishly challenging and immensely clever X.27тАУ29, as well as another poet with the same patronymic, namely Vasukr╠еt V─Бsukra, one possible author of X.20тАУ26, another set of well-crafted hymns. Moreover, the final verse of X.65 (15) and the final two of X.66 (14тАУ15) mention Vasiс╣гс╣нha and the Vasiс╣гс╣нhas, and both hymns end with the Vasiс╣гс╣нha clan refrain familiar from Maс╣Зс╕Нala VII.

Griffith

Thus hath the thoughtful sage the son of Plati, praised you, O Aaiti and all Adityas.
Men are made rich by those who are Immortal: the Heavenly Folk have been extolled by Gaya.
